Less than ten days after this incident, there was a surge of riots among the Korean residents there. According to the results of the investigation by the Chinese authorities, the two youths who entered the country were indeed suspected of instigating the Korean residents to plan the riots. Therefore, they have separately ordered their subordinates to be on guard." (August 19th)

They arrived in Fushun at 1:35 PM and inspected at 3:05 PM. They left Fushun at 6:40 PM on the 22nd and arrived in Shenyang at 8:00 PM, staying at the Yamato Hotel. (August 21st)

Shantou Hurricane Disrupts Transportation 76

Guangsheng Ship Mishaps

Shantou Correspondence: Since the 13th, Shantou has been overcast with thick clouds in the sky. White waves have been surging at sea, and ships have been forbidden from going out. According to the Customs report, a hurricane has occurred in the Ningbo and Wenzhou sea areas, and Weisheng has hit a reef. Guangsheng, which departed from Shanghai to Shantou, has gone missing midway. The wind has been even stronger on the 14th and 15th. According to the Customs report, the wind is at 23 degrees 21 minutes north latitude and 16 degrees 40 minutes east longitude, located between Shantou and Shanwei. Large ships are anchored and dare not export. That night, the wind and rain raged, water flooded the streets, and the Han River also rose several feet. By the 17th, the dangerous period had passed, and the ships began to sail out, but the sea was still rough. Several small boats capsized, and two houses collapsed in the city. Many wired poles were blown down. The losses in Chaoshan are very small, but the Guangsheng has not yet arrived in Shantou. Jardine Matheson sent Zesheng and Hesheng to search on the 15th, but there was no news. It was not until yesterday that it was confirmed that the ship had unfortunately sunk in the storm. Jining's Unprecedented Flood, Outside the City Becomes a Lake 77

Jining Correspondence: Jining, Shandong Province, straddles the Grand Canal and is a prosperous county in western Shandong. This year, before the start of the dog days, when the autumn crops were being cultivated, there was heavy rain, and many autumn crops were flooded. After entering the dog days, the weather was not clear, and the climate was cool, which was very different from the past. Then, the twelve consecutive depressions in the upper reaches of Jiaxiang, Juye, Shanxian, Caoxian, Dingtao, Heze, and Chengwu counties burst, and the water overflowed and poured into Jining, causing the east, west, and other parts of the city to be submerged in water. Recently, the weather has turned hot, and it has been raining continuously. In addition, the water from the Wen River, Si River, Guang River, and Fu River has risen sharply at the same time and rushed from the east, its momentum is fierce and cannot be protected, causing the land east and north of the city to be flooded. Now, the outside of the city is a vast expanse of water, which has become a lake. The ship cannot travel out of the city gate. The water on the plain is about four or five feet, and the water in the deep depressions is even deeper. In addition to the fields being flooded, houses have collapsed and people have drowned. It has not been possible to investigate clearly. It is truly an unprecedented disaster. (August 21st)

Starting today (the 25th), those who are found to be privately smuggling Japanese goods, if the value is above 5,000 yuan, will have the words "Traitor" tattooed on their face; those above 2,500 yuan will wear a paper hat and parade through the streets for seven days; those above 1,000 yuan will parade through the streets for three days; those above 100 yuan will parade through the streets for one day; those below 100 yuan will be fined the price of the goods, and if they are unable to pay, they will be sentenced to detention. Repeat offenders will be punished twice as severely, and those who commit the crime three times will be punished as counter-revolutionaries. Those who undermine the anti-Japanese work will have the words "Traitorous People" tattooed on their faces and will be sent to the judicial authorities for punishment. Lake Bandits Flee to Xin'an Town: Xin'an Town in the county's 13th district is located on the shore of Taihu Lake, with many diverging waterways. On March 12th, two bandit boats arrived in Xin'an Town, intending to kidnap Dr. Hui Ming. Fortunately, the villagers were well-prepared, and the lake bandits fled back to Taihu Lake. After the incident, Hui immediately moved to the city, and the others with some wealth could not sleep peacefully either. Unexpectedly, a few days ago, several bandit boats suddenly arrived at the Sha Dun port, about three miles south of the Gao Dun port, and the bandits went ashore one after another. Most of the residents there make a living by fishing, and they were all terrified and did not dare to fish. There was originally a detachment of the county police team there, but it has now been transferred to another location, so the defense is very weak. Fortunately, the bandits have not made any other unusual movements. The bandit boats that suddenly arrived this time were due to the active bandit suppression in Huzhou, which sealed off all eight ports along the lake, including Pan Lou Port, Luo Lou Port, Da Lou Port, Shen Lou Port, Tang Jia Port, and An Port, causing the bandits to be unable to hide and flee to Xin'an.

Xiangtai Leather Goods Store Suddenly Goes Bankrupt: Xiangtai Leather Goods Store in Shuyuan Lane, in the city, has been in business since last August for less than a year. It owes customers and merchants seven or eight thousand yuan, which has led to a shortage of funds and sudden bankruptcy. Manager Zhu Yixian not only does not try to remedy the situation, but also avoids meeting people. None of the shareholders has come forward to deal with the matter. All the employees in the store have also left, leaving only a few apprentices inside to guard the store door. Therefore, the creditors, Yun Yujiandzhuang and Hua Xin Yi, two cloth factories, and Jiu Sheng and other firms, yesterday sent a joint official letter to the county chamber of commerce, requesting that the leather goods industry be invited to seal up the store's inventory and property, and requesting that a statement be published in the newspaper, warning all the shareholders of Xiangtai and manager Zhu Yixian to come forward to deal with the matter within a limited time. After the Chamber of Commerce approved the letter, it has already been approved for handling.

Careless Refueling Causes Tragic Burning of Mother and Daughter: Luo Wuda, a villager in Huangniwan, about four miles south of Zhangjing Bridge in the 7th district (Huai Shang Shi), is over fifty years old. His son, Shunquan, is over thirty years old. The father and son are both farmers. Shunquan's wife, Yu, is thirty-two years old and has a son and a daughter. The son's name is Xiaobao, five years old, and the daughter's name is Suzhen, twelve years old. At eight o'clock in the evening the day before, Yu saw that the fuel in the kerosene lamp was running out and was about to go out, so she took the lamp to the door of the room, opened the kerosene tank, and was about to refuel when, unexpectedly, sparks from the lamp fell into the oil tank and immediately caught fire. Seeing that the fire had started, Yu turned around and entered the room to try to save her son, but mistakenly grabbed her daughter Suzhen. Just as she was about to rush out of the door through the fire, she stumbled over the threshold and the kerosene completely spilled, causing the mother and daughter to be tragically burned to death. Later, Wuda and his son learned about the situation and went inside to put out the fire, which was extinguished, preventing the houses, beds, trunks, and other items from being damaged, which was very fortunate.

Special Article

Forests and Water Conservancy (Li Yingong) 89

There are many recent events that can be used as evidence to prove the importance of afforestation and flood prevention. Yu the Great's success in controlling the floods relied on the ancient trees that covered the sky and the living things that filled the earth at that time. The torrential rain that fell was immediately reduced by half, and the situation was quickly brought under control. It was not like the later generations who only opened up agricultural land, resulting in a reduction in the area of wild forests and bushes, and it is no wonder that floods occurred frequently and were constantly recorded in history. The southern region of France is mostly mountainous. At first, at the beginning of the 19th century, the area of mixed pasture forests and indiscriminate logging expanded year by year. As a result, mountain floods broke out and quicksand spread throughout the country, causing great harm. Since 1841, the engineer Shuhe published a plan for "Fundamentally Treating the Disease by Operating the Forest," followed by the forester Montesquieu's firm statement that to save floods, it is necessary to manage water, prevent sand, and build protective forests. The government then drafted a compulsory protective afforestation law, raising more than three million in funding annually and appointing a supervisor to complete the work within a limited time. Since then, the floods have been greatly reduced, and the southern provinces of Upper Arleber and Pu Arleber have benefited the most from the forest. Farmers not only do not object to the purchase of private land, but also request the government to add their fields to the protective forest. The human-protected forest is also a successful example of afforestation and flood prevention.

Forests and water conservancy have never been noticed in our country, and few people have discussed them. Although the entire territory includes the Pearl River, Yangtze River, Huai Si, Yellow River, and Heilongjiang River basins, the area in square miles lacks investigation. We should classify and grade the land's highlands (hunting grounds or parts suitable for forest cultivation), grasslands (natural forest and pasture), and lowlands (most of the agricultural land and abandoned land along the water) to classify their uses. It is rare not to feel that forests and water conservancy are interrelated everywhere. As for the utilization of Hou Sheng, it also includes the recent rainfall in the capital on July 4th and 5th, which amounted to 227.1 millimeters, which is about nine inches. As a result, it has not stopped for ten days and has become a rare disaster that occurs only once in fifty years, which makes people realize that this problem needs to be studied. Especially today, protective forests are unheard of, and it is not logical to talk about water conservancy. Usually, provinces along the river have water conservancy bureaus, and provinces along the Yellow River and the Grand Canal also have officials in charge of river engineering affairs. What exactly are their duties? It is confusing to many people. The heavy expenditure of the year is equal to the empty hen's alarm to the dam and the appropriation of funds for emergency rescue, which is enough to make people laugh. It can be seen that the general public is too indifferent to academic forest management and forest benefits. Moreover, the meaning of protective forests is very broad, and water management only accounts for one of its effects. Wind prevention, sand prevention, tsunami prevention, etc., are all based on the needs of local conditions, and the operating procedures are changed accordingly, which cannot be adhered to one set of rules. However, not lightly harvesting and only selective logging are its common principles. The branches and leaves of the trees fall under the forest to provide fertilizer and improve the soil's power. During the rainy season, they help the roots to retain the rapid torrents. In peacetime, they complete the function of conserving water resources. It is also the same. Therefore, firewood is absolutely prohibited in all forestry. In the countryside of our country, there is a great lack of fuel. Banning firewood in forest areas is considered a great rebellion in the environment. Protective benefits are great, and banning firewood is small. How can they know? Therefore, without laws and regulations to force the gentry to publicize, there is no one day to enter the right track.

In other countries, hydraulic engineers can often set up independent schemes and create plans that are not surprising. Only our great rivers and plains have a clear situation. Taking the Yangtze River as an example, the mountains in the upper reaches are connected to each other, and nine out of ten of them are bald. So far, there is still no strong public order to afforest them. On both sides of the river, people do not automatically plant trees to protect the embankment. Mountain rain washes away, and sediment accumulates on the bottom of the river every year. Once the water rises, there is no fear of the dam collapsing and flooding the fields. Therefore, in the past, the country only felt a shortage of wood, such as the market being filled with American Douglas fir, California cypress, Japanese spruce, Japanese elm, oak, Philippine white lauan, red lauan, Philippine apitong, West Australian mahogany, Northwest Siberian mahogany, Russian red pine, etc. The outflow of rights and interests has now progressed to the problem of people and animals being flooded, which is even more related. Every few years, they want to experience it once, and the feeling may even be worse. This is inevitable and can be asserted. The forest referred to in the wooden article is different from the economic specialty of ordinary forestry. Because general forestry relies on highlands and grassland planning to transform a vast wasteland into production, diligently seeking long-term quantities and making ten times the profit, this is just to make the best use of the lowlands (based on the county) and roughly draft the following entry methods: 1. Survey and management of forest management. It is necessary to be clear about the local situation, soil properties, and depth, wind direction, wind power, and local tree species before appropriate techniques can be applied.

2. Survey and mapping including measuring the land, purchasing land, registering official wastelands, and preparing budgets (roughly speaking, the cost of raising seedlings and planting broad-leaved tree seedlings is twice that of coniferous trees).

3. The operating plan divides the annual limited planting volume based on the number of acres and establishes a management procedure to avoid interruption.

Attached is a discussion on the selection of trees for afforestation on embankments or lowlands. Please list them: (1) Swamp Walnut, also known as Feng Yang, belongs to the walnut family. The reason for the difference is that it is a naked species. There are seven kinds of swamp walnuts, and China occupies five of them, so the distribution is particularly far away. They can all grow in streams and wet places, like fertile soil, and have fast growth. If they are in alluvial land, they will flourish even more. The wood is similar to the linden tree, white, light, and soft, for use in utensils, and is especially suitable for making wooden clogs and book boxes. It can also be used as a carving.

(2) Weeping Willow, Common Willow, Qi Willow, and Stream Willow are all not afraid of water. It is very easy to propagate using cuttings, and the survival rate is the highest. Weeping Willow can also be planted by burying large camellias. The branches on both sides of the long river in the West Lake Su Causeway and the Yangzhou Ping Mountain Hall hang down, and the entrance is closed and decorated with beautiful scenery. Although it is submerged for a long time, it does not matter. The wood has value.

(3) White Poplar Willow, produced in Hebei, Jiangsu, Hubei, Sichuan, and other provinces. It is especially common between 4,000 and 7,000 in the Minjiang River basin in Sichuan, but it is usually scattered. The trunk is straight and very beautiful. People in the capital often call it Nanjing White Poplar. It is very easy to reproduce, and the growth rate is fast. There are many fishermen and houses planted beside Xuanwu Lake, and they are also seen mixed with lakes, which are high above the treetops and cute in green. The wood is suitable for various uses. (4) White Poplar is produced from Hebei and Shaanxi to the south to Jiangsu and Zhejiang. The tree shape is neat and beautiful, and the height and length can reach six feet. The bark is blue-white, and the old tree is dark and cracked. The leaves are triangular, with different sizes at the pointed ends, with light hair on the surface or smooth, and white on the inner side, with dense hair, so it is called White Poplar. This tree is quite difficult to live with cuttings. It is suitable to cut off the branches in winter, bury them in the cellar, dig them out in early spring, cut them into appropriate lengths, and dig trenches in the garden before inserting them. Fill with mud and then insert. After that, you must water them frequently to avoid drying. The material is excellent.

(5) Chinese Parasol Tree, also known as Qing Tong, is easily cultivated by seed propagation in China, and the old roots have strong re-emergence ability, but the top buds are afraid of frost, and it is less obstructive after the early years. Can survive in water-surplus soil. The ancient saying is: The Parasol Tree grows on the Autumn River, which can be played with.

(6) White Birch likes moist soil and can reach three or four feet in height. The skin is thin, white, and easy to peel off. There are about thirty-two kinds of Chinese products, some of which belong to small trees. The wood is white and dense and is used for appliances, and the smaller ones can be used as firewood (7) Wu Yue is produced in Sichuan, Guizhou, Guangxi, Hubei, Hunan, Anhui, Zhejiang, Fujian, and other provinces. I have seen people in Zhejiang sparsely planting this in the lowlands along the lake, harvesting seeds to extract oil and wax, and doubling their profits. After the by-products are taken, the slag can be used as fertilizer, which is also a good fertilizer. When the tree is old, it will bear fruit and can produce more seeds. The newly reclaimed low-lying land along the Jiujiang River in Dongliuqiupu, Anhui is also very lush (8) Xiao Xuan Mu, mistakenly called French Parasol, another kind of P·OCCIDENTALIS are both ancient tree species and fossils have been found in Europe, North America, and the northern part of Asia. Suitable for all kinds of wind and soil, can withstand coal smoke, and is not afraid of alkaline soil. Propagation generally uses cuttings. The branches with reddish color have a higher survival rate. After many experiments by the world, it is generally believed that it is a tree of lowlands and water. The wood is quite like beech, with rich texture and color, and the effect is not limited to one way.

In addition, you can add water-loving trees in each county as appropriate. Use GROUPSYSTEM for experimentation, and write down their growth status separately to serve as a standard for future preservation or elimination. After several years, expand the scope of operations to determine the operating plan. If the counties follow it earnestly and the general hub of forestry administration supervises it, then water conservancy may be possible. In addition, this year's flood should be recognized by the people of the country as a result of deforestation. They can use labor relief or military labor to mobilize the group to do their best to address the urgent task of afforestation and flood prevention, so Yingong's draft of this article is not false.

Letter

Letter from Li Bin, Linping Station Master of Shanghai-Hangzhou Road 90

Dear Sir, Recently, I read a report in the local communication Hangzhou Communication column of your newspaper on the 17th of this month, which stated that the station master was dismissed for a gambling case at the station. This is not in line with the facts. It has been found that Lai Chen and the other two were arrested for suspicion of gambling outside. The station master temporarily guaranteed them. They were transferred to the Hangzhou Land Court for interrogation the day before yesterday. The interrogation revealed that the station master was not involved and was not summoned. If he had been gambling with them at the time, how could he have been a guarantor? Therefore, whether it is extremely obvious. As for the Road Bureau ordering Li to be dismissed and deducting three months' salary as a warning, it is even more unfounded. The station master is still working in Lin and there is no such bureau order. I do not know what the visiting reporter based his statement on, which is of great importance to his reputation. I am specially writing to request a correction to clarify the truth. Education News

Important News

Record of the 16th Annual Meeting of the China Science Society (2) 91

The 16th annual meeting of the China Science Society was held in Zhenjiang. The situation of the opening ceremony on the first day was reported in yesterday's newspaper. Now, the situation on the 23rd will be recorded as follows:

(1) Taking a boat to Jiaoshan

After the banquet held by the provincial government at Pinfang on the evening of the 22nd, some members returned to the mountain by boat, while the rest went to the Dahua Hotel by the river. After breakfast at 8 a.m. on the 23rd, they went to the car ferry pier and took a small steamer to Jiaoshan. Although the weather on land was sultry and hot that day, after the anchor was raised, the waves were calm and the wind blew across the water, making it cool and pleasant. After a short boat trip, this majestic green peak on the river was in sight. The group happily went ashore.

(2) Council Meeting

The council meeting was held at 9 a.m. in Zhenjiang Pavilion, chaired by Wang Jiliang. He reported on the opening of the meeting, saying briefly that it was rare to have so many members at the council meeting today. He said that he would report the following matters and leave matters such as elections for later discussion. He also read telegrams from Society members Hu Shih, Ding Wenjiang, Weng Wenhao, Zhao Yuanren, and Shu Yong from Peiping, stating that they could not attend this annual meeting and expressing their apologies. Then, the

Board of Directors Report (represented by Secretary-General Yang Xiaoshu) briefly stated that many things had been done in the past year, and now the most important ones were selected for a brief report: (1) The establishment of Society member associations in three locations: A, Hangzhou; B, Qingdao; C, Suzhou. Together with the original five locations in Beijing, Ping, Shanghai, Wuhan, and Shenyang, there were now eight locations. The Chongqing Society member association was still in the process of being established. (2) The completion of two new buildings: A, the Shanghai Mingfu Library; B, the Beijing Biological Research Institute; C, Initially, it was intended to hold an arts and crafts exhibition, but due to the large scale, it was not easy to organize at once, so a version exhibition was held in Shanghai. Mr. Cai contributed a lot, and many of the precious versions were borrowed by Mr. Cai privately from various sources. There were more than 100 Song editions, and many Six Dynasties editions. Yuan, Ming, and Qing editions were needless to say. In addition, famous foreign editions and precious handwritten books were also borrowed. Modern printing, such as various versions from the Commercial Press and China Bookstore, were also displayed. The exhibition lasted for six days, and more than 5,000 people attended. (3) This year, the Society admitted five permanent members, 116 ordinary members, and six associate members, for a total of 1,289 members. (The addresses of more than 850 people are unknown.) (4) Addition of irregular publications to transmit news among Society members. 345 letters were received during the year. (5) The circulation of the Science Magazine published by the Society has been increasing year by year, which shows that the public has a considerable interest in science. It is estimated that 155 copies were subscribed to in the 17th year, 422 copies in the 18th year, and 594 copies in the 19th year. In addition to the Science Magazine, 247 copies of other publications were sold in the 17th year, 351 copies in the 18th year, and 394 copies in the 19th year, which also showed considerable progress. (6) Essay award, the scope of the essay was physics and other subjects, and there were seven universities applying, etc. Then, the

Accounting Report (Zhou Zijing) briefly stated that the accounting revenue and expenditure had been prepared in writing and distributed to all members. (The written report was too long to be recorded.) The account was reviewed by Gu Jigao and He Zhongliu, two members publicly recommended by the Society. The total revenue was briefly stated as follows: (1) Previous balance: 12,097.71 yuan in foreign currency and 1 pound in gold. (2) Revenue for this year: 74,006.69 yuan and 16,977 taels of silver. (3) Expenditure for this year: 92,795.47 yuan in foreign currency and 16,977 taels of silver. (4) Balance: 13,308.93 yuan in foreign currency and 8 taels of silver. Then, the

Biological Research Institute Report (Bing Lushan) briefly stated that since last year, long-term expeditions and investigations of flora and fauna in various coastal areas have been carried out, and many kinds of flora and fauna specimens have been collected and compiled into the Institute. Last year's research papers were divided into two departments, including three articles in the botany department and ten articles in the zoology department, totaling six volumes. The most gratifying thing this year was that temporary funding was obtained from the China Cultural Foundation to build a new house. In order to seek long-term academic progress, various equipment had to be slightly prepared. The old houses for studios and specimens were no longer sufficient, so adding a house was imperative. This new building was completed at the end of this year, including a two-story building with a total of 36 rooms. The assets in the Research Institute, such as books, specimens, instruments, medicines, physiology, histology, experimental zoology, etc., were all moved to the new house. As for the research on anatomy and taxonomy, and the preparation of stripped and immersed specimens, etc., they were still in the old house. The working conditions of the animal and plant departments in the past year are described separately as follows:

(Animal Department) 1. Full-time staff: Bingzhi, Wang Jiaji, Wang Qinfu, Zhang Mengwen, Zhou Weicheng, Hao Shixiang, He Xirui, Jia Qinyin, Feng Zhanru, Liu Zigang, Chen Jinsheng. 2. Part-time staff: Fang Bingwen, Chen Yi, Wu Gongxian, Yang, Wu Changsheng, Fan Desheng, Huang Qilin. 3. Research results that have been published: Distribution of motor areas of the guinea pig brain, a new species of turtle, record of abdominal hair insects, Xiamen giant frog, revision of new genera and related genera of Chinese cyprinid fishes, research on several fishes in the upper reaches of the Yangtze River, a new species of Fuzhou sea fish, life history of white rats, research on three-bodied chicken embryos, a new species of Sichuan cyprinid fishes, and two new species of weaving hair insects. 4. Research papers that have been printed: A brief record of Nanjing animals, muscle anatomy of the head of Xiamen lizards, fish of Fuzhou, a record of Nanjing amphibians, a brief record of Sichuan amphibians, a brief record of Sichuan earthworms, changes in the stomach of goldfish in spring and winter, development of the reaction area of goldfish, changes in frog kidney cells during the four seasons. 5. Research in progress: Investigation of echinoderms along the Chinese coast, anatomy of lizard tongues, investigation of ostracods along the southeast coast of China, reaction potential of guinea pig limbs, appearance of the cerebral cortex when stimulated by electricity, continued investigation of Nanjing protozoa, investigation of protozoa in the lower reaches of the Yangtze River, the effect of iodine on the schizogony of paramecium, anatomy of turtle muscles, research on Yantai marine fish, snakes of Nanjing, a brief record of Sichuan snakes, life history of goldfish, anatomy of centipede trachea, investigation of Nanjing spiders, growth of white rat cerebellum (Pan Genqi) cells, growth of white rat cerebral cortex cells, investigation of Nanjing rotifers, investigation of Nanjing crickets. 6. Collection and utilization of specimens: In June last year, staff were sent down the Yangtze River from Nanjing to Wusong to collect submerged fish and various birds along the river, led by Mr. Wang Qinfu. They went to Zhenjiang, Wuxi, Suzhou, Yixing, Kunshan, etc., and the obtained specimens were sent to Professor Shou Zhenfei of the Jing Sheng Biological Survey Institute in Peiping and Dr. Zhang Chunlin of the University of Paris for research. About 600 kinds of bird specimens were also sent to Mr. Shou. Snake specimens were provided for research by Mr. Fang Bingwen and Mr. Zhang Mengwen in the Institute. The old snake and amphibian specimens were sorted out by the two gentlemen. The fish specimens collected from Yantai were sorted out by Mr. Wang Qinfu and Mr. Wu Xianwen. The echinoderms from the southeastern provinces have been classified and studied by Dr. Bing Nongshan. In addition, earthworms, flatworms, roundworms, etc., were studied by Mr. Chen Yi and Mr. Xu Xifan. Mr. Fang Bingwen collected Nanjing spiders and paid attention to fish, frogs, and snakes. Mr. Wang Qinfu was in charge of centipedes, and Mr. He Xirui was in charge of orthopterans. Ms. Qian Qin Su Mei collected a large number of butterfly specimens and sent them to the British Museum, and now they have been transferred to Mr. Huang Qilin. 7. Purchase of books and instruments: A, entertainment items and instruments, 430 bottles of old medicines were stored, and recently 130 bottles were purchased. In terms of instruments, a high-power microscope, a balance, and 1,000 glass parts were newly purchased. B, about 114 kinds of books have been obtained by donation and exchange, and about 30 kinds of journals have been ordered. More than 700 international publications have been donated.

The results of the election of directors were reported: Weng Wenhao, Bing Nongshan, Yang Xingfo, Hu Gangfu, and Zhao Yuanren were elected as directors. Ye Qisun, Qian Chongshu, and Zhang Zigao were elected as alternate directors.

A list of important resolutions was made. After the report, the proposals were discussed, and the resolutions are recorded as follows: (1) Accept the accounting statement (resolution)

Sports

Seven Hundred People Revel, China Wins Rotary Cup Finals Qualification 92

The last two singles matches were indeed all won | 3 to 2 eliminated Canada

Jiang Daozhang won three straight against Litt | Not difficult

Qiu Feihai won Deffau after five sets | Extremely dangerous

Finals against Japan start on the 28th

Everyone was happy. Qiu Feihai and Jiang Daozhang lived up to expectations, winning all against the two Canadian singles players. The Chinese team won the Rotary Cup World Tennis Finals qualification. Canada initially led 2 to 1, but was eliminated by China with a score of 2 to 3. Jiang Daozhang's victory over Litt was not difficult, but Qiu Feihai's victory over Deffau was full of ups and downs and dangerous situations. More than seven hundred people watched with bated breath. Qiu Feihai's hard-fought five-set victory can be said to be fortunate. The finals against Japan are scheduled to begin on the 28th.

Jiang Daozhang Wins Litt 93

| Three straight sets very easy |

| Canada first lost |

Jiang Daozhang (China) (6-4) (6-2) (6-3) Litt (Canada)

Jiang Daozhang won three straight against Litt. The Chinese team first regained one point, tying the score. Litt was far from Jiang's opponent yesterday. The audience was very happy and gratified to see Jiang's successive victories.

Smooth sailing, Litt served, Jiang Daozhang had smooth sailing and won four games in a row. Litt regained three games, and Jiang won the first set 6-4. The second set started, and Jiang Daozhang still used a very powerful block and hit the corners. Although Litt was a good net player, he could not get close to the net. After 4-1, Jiang won the second set 6-2. After Jiang won two sets, the victory was set. Litt served again and won one game. Jiang then won three games in a row, winning 3-2 and then 6-3, making it three straight.

Good luck, Jiang performed much better than usual yesterday, very smoothly and extraordinarily. The balls he hit were just over the net, sharp and cut. Litt could only see the net. The cross-court shots were also extremely accurate. Litt could not defend the net. It was also good luck. Although, Litt's skills were not comparable to Jiang's.

Qiu Feihai Loses to Deffau 94

| Two hours of worry |

| Five sets to win |

(2-6)

Qiu Feihai (China) (6-2) Deffau (Canada)

(6-3)

(3-6)

(6-4)

After Jiang Daozhang won against Litt, the fate of China and Canada depended on who won between Qiu Feihai and Deffau. After the Jiang-Litt match, Qiu was leading Deffau 2-1. In an instant, Deffau also regained one set, making it 2-2. In the last set, at the critical moment of life and death, General Qiu used his life, and indeed won 6-4. The Chinese team then won the finals qualification.

The weather changed. When Qiu and Deffau started the match, the north wind was blowing wildly and the sky was overcast. Qiu Feihai served, and lost four games in a row. Deffau went to the net to block and kill every game, guarding the pass. Seeing that blocking was sure to be killed, Qiu tried to hit a high ball to get over it, but the close shots touched the net, and the high balls went out of bounds, and he was at a loss. 4-1, 5-2, and lost 2-6. The audience was shocked to see this situation. The weather also changed, with drizzling rain and wind all over the field.

Sudden turning point. At the start of the second set Qiu Feihai lost two more games. Qiu was lamenting his lack of luck, when the wind and rain stopped, and from then on the situation turned around. Seeing the failure of the high ball, Qiu knew that he still had to rely on fierce shots. So he ignored Deffau's net defense and shot fiercely at the corners. The ball was low and fast. Deffau raised his racket to return, but touched the net repeatedly and hit the ball out of bounds with force. Once this road was opened, Qiu Feihai's path was smooth, winning nine consecutive games. In the second set, he won six consecutive games, showing Deffau some color.

The hearts of the people settled. At the start of the third set Qiu won three more games, so a total of nine games. Although Qiu was fierce, when the opportunity came, he gently chopped the ball, which landed in front of the net and did not bounce up. Sometimes close, sometimes far, the skills were miraculous. Deffau recovered the score to 2-3. Qiu was 5-2, 6-3, and won the third set again. He led with a total of 2-1, and the hearts of the people were settled.

Loss of opportunity again. It was hoped that Qiu would win one more set, then the victory would be set. How could he know that when Deffau served, Qiu lost three games in a row. He barely picked up one game, and Deffau was in a very advantageous position again at 5-1, and won the fourth set 6-3. Qiu lost the opportunity to win again here. With the loss of this set, the score was 2-2. Everyone knew that Qiu's physical strength was weak, and they were very worried about his victory in the fifth set.

Go home with peace of mind. The success or failure, victory or defeat, all depended on this last set. Everyone looked at each other, very worried. Deffau served, Qiu got it, and Deffau also won one game. Then Qiu won two consecutive games, leading with 3-1, and was 60% confident, half relieved. At 5-3, Deffau served, Deffau suddenly attacked from left and right, recovering the score to 5-4. The worry came again. If it became 5-5, there would be more trouble. Good luck and fortune came, Qiu won 6-4 and was overjoyed. Two hours of worry were finally over, and he went home with peace of mind.

Shanghai Municipal Games Begin Registration 97

From today until 4:00 p.m. on September 7th

| Registration procedures and registration instructions were released yesterday |

The 2nd Shanghai Municipal Games, which will be held from September 12th to 18th, will start registration today. The various sections of the competition department and the competition committees are working hard. The registration procedures and various competition registration instructions have been decided and released by Shen Siliang, director of the competition department, and others, as follows:

Registration Procedures 98

(1) Registration will start today and end at 4:00 p.m. on September 7th. No applications will be accepted after the deadline.

(2) Registration location: Registration Office of the Municipal Games at the Municipal Education Bureau (3) Registration applicants, whether groups or individuals, must request or pick up the registration form from the registration office, fill it out, and submit it to the registration office.

(4) After registration, no individual or group may withdraw halfway or fail to attend the on-site competition. Violators will be subject to penalties separately determined by the committee, such as not being allowed to participate in various sports organized by the city in the future, and notifying the affiliated schools or institutions to punish them, etc.

Various Registration Instructions 99

(1) Track and Field

(1) Both men's and women's track and field competitions are based on individuals and are not divided into groups.

(2) Each person can participate in a maximum of four events for men and three events for women.

(3) Those who participate in the decathlon and pentathlon cannot participate in the pentathlon, and those who participate in the pentathlon cannot participate in the decathlon.

(4) Track and field competitions will be held on the first and second days, and pentathlon and decathlon competitions will be held on the third and fourth days.

(2) Football

(1) Based on groups, each team can register a maximum of 20 people, including the administrator.

(2) School football teams must be signed and sealed by the principal and the director of physical education before they can be registered.

(3) Non-school football teams must have a considerable history before they can be registered, and the standing committee of the football has the right to review whether the registered football teams are qualified.

(4) If the number of participating teams is four or more, a knockout system will be used for the competition. If there are only three teams, a single round-robin system will be used. If there are only two teams, a three-game two-win system will be used.

(3) Basketball

(1) Both men's and women's basketball are based on groups. Each men's basketball team can register a maximum of 11 people, and each women's basketball team can register a maximum of 13 people, including the administrator. (2) School basketball teams must be signed and sealed by the principal and the director of physical education before they can be registered.

(3) Non-school basketball teams must have a considerable history before they can be registered, and the standing committee of the basketball team has the right to review whether the registered basketball teams are qualified.

(4) If the number of participating teams is six or more, a knockout system will be used for the competition. If there are three to five teams, a single round-robin system will be used. If there are only two teams, a three-game two-win system will be used to determine the winner.

(4) Tennis

(1) Singles are based on individuals, doubles are based on groups, and are divided into men's singles, women's singles, men's doubles, and women's doubles.

(2) For men's singles and doubles, except for the semi-finals and finals, which use a five-game three-win system, the other weeks all use a three-game two-win system.

(3) All women's competitions use a three-game two-win system.

(4) All contestants should arrive at the venue on time according to the date scheduled by the association. Those who are more than 15 minutes late will be considered to have forfeited.

(5) All matches will use "Laide Edison" brand tennis balls, which will be provided by the association.

(6) The competition will be held on grass or hard court, which will be decided by the committee.

(5) Volleyball

(1) Both men's and women's volleyball are based on groups. Each men's volleyball team can register a maximum of 15 people, and each women's volleyball team can register a maximum of 17 people, including the administrator.

(2) School teams must be signed and sealed by the principal and the director of physical education before they can be registered.

(3) Each school team must have a considerable history before it can be registered, and the volleyball committee has the right to review whether the registered teams are qualified.

(4) If there are more than eight teams participating in the competition, a knockout system will be used. If there are three to seven teams, a single round-robin system will be used. If there are only two teams, a five-game three-win system will be used.

(6) Baseball

(1) Based on groups, each team can register a maximum of 15 people, including the administrator.

(2) All teams that are organized and willing to participate in the competition are welcome. (3) If the number of participating teams is four or more, a knockout system will be used for the competition. If there are only three teams, a single round-robin system will be used. If there are only two teams, a three-game two-win system will be used.

(7) Swimming

(1) Both men's and women's swimming are based on individuals. Each man can participate in a maximum of four events, and each woman can participate in a maximum of three events.

(2) All applicants for the competition, regardless of gender, must have a doctor's certificate to check for eye diseases and other infectious diseases, etc., and submit it to Ling Xitao, chairman of the swimming committee, before the competition.

(8) Race Walking

Race walking is listed as a performance event, but the association will also award prizes to the top three in order to promote it. As for the half-distance and route, it will be announced after consultation between the association's administrator and Shi Youhui.

(Note) The national martial arts competition is organized by the Shanghai National Martial Arts Hall. Please register at the hall in Zhabei.

Local News

The Second Big Wind is Coming Again 100

The customs fired cannons to warn that Jianghai ships were suspended

For nearly a week, the local area has been scorching hot, and the mercury has often been between 96 and 97 degrees. Until the day before yesterday, the wind was calm, and the autumn sun was even more terrible. But in the morning, the wind picked up and dark clouds chased, and the weather suddenly became cooler. It is said that the hurricane in the Pacific Ocean has advanced to the East China Sea and is blowing towards the coast of Jiangsu and Zhejiang. According to the warning from the Xujiahui Observatory at 11 a.m. yesterday, at that time the hurricane had passed Naha and was only 600 kilometers away from Shanghai, moving northwest and northwest by west, approaching the coast between Shanghai and Wenzhou. It was expected to land before this morning, but according to the observatory's forecast at 4:30 p.m., the wind direction has turned to the northwest by west, approaching the coast of Wenzhou and Taizhou. It is feared that it will still follow the previous route and blow through the Oujiang River basin, or it may not pass Shanghai. At 9 p.m. last night, a special warning was issued, saying that a very large hurricane is now slowly blowing through the East China Sea, and due to the pressure in northern China and Japan, it has turned to the northwest by west. The East China Sea and the Wusongkou to the coast of Taiwan are turbulent, and there are also cyclones.

The customs notified the shipping industry that at 1:30 p.m. yesterday, the Shanghai Jianghai Customs hoisted a strong wind signal and a warning black ball at the intersection of Avenue Edward VII, and immediately notified the shipping companies to order the sea ships in Shanghai that had not yet left the port to suspend sailing temporarily, so that they could stay in the Huangpu River to avoid the wind and avoid accidents. At 4:30 p.m., the Pudong flag station also hoisted a black wind ball and fired a cannon to warn at the same time.

Near-sea ships were suspended. The location and direction of this big wind were similar to the last time, so yesterday, the Shanghai-Ningbo liners of the Taikoo and Ning Shao companies, such as the Xin Beijing, announced the suspension of sailing after receiving the customs warning. The passengers who had boarded the ship纷纷 returned their tickets and went back, and changed to leave the port tomorrow. The Xin Jiangtian and Ning Xing ships, which came from Ningbo, were also telegraphed yesterday to avoid the wind in Ningbo and not to come for the time being. The Shanghai-Taiwan class, Wenzhou-Haimen class, and other near-sea routes all suspended sailing at noon yesterday and stayed in Shanghai to avoid the wind.

The Nan Hua liners delayed sailing. The local shipping companies, punished by the danger of encountering the wind last time, are now extra cautious. The Taikoo Nan Hua liners, such as the Suiyang and the Nisshin Rosan Maru, have all delayed their departure time and will not sail until the wind subsides this morning. The Yangtze River ships have also postponed their departure time. If the wind does not subside this morning, they will decide not to sail.

Small boats in the Huangpu River avoid the wind. Since yesterday afternoon, the tide in the Huangpu River has risen sharply. The small barges and sampans on the river surface have stopped loading and unloading goods and carrying passengers across the river. In the evening, the small steamers also stopped running, and the civilian ships sailed into the Suzhou River to avoid the wind.

The last hurricane caused a maritime disaster. A total of four ships were wrecked in the first hurricane. Jardine Matheson had a Weisen who touched a reef and drowned one person. The rest were rescued and came to Shanghai. Then, the Guang Sheng Lun was sunk by the wind and waves, and all the passengers and employees fell into the sea. Only three people were rescued. The families of the victims have been coming to the company for days to inquire about the truth. It was not until yesterday that news came from Fuzhou, saying that the Guang Sheng Lun encountered a strong wind and the hull touched a reef. The whole ship sank in two hours. None of the passengers, crew members, and sailors on board were spared and all fell into the sea. Only one stoker, one sailor, and one cook were able to float on the sea after falling into the sea. After 36 hours, they were rescued by a fishing boat, and then boarded a wooden boat to Fuzhou. On the 24th of this month, the Jardine Matheson in Fuzhou and the British Consul sent the three people to the Wanzhou ship of the Sanbei Company and sent them back to Shanghai. It is expected to arrive on Thursday. The truth about the Guang Sheng Lun's accident and the number of deaths on the whole ship (at least it should be in the hundreds) will be clear after the three people arrive in Shanghai.

News from Various Sectors on Disaster Relief Yesterday 101

The Enthusiastic Automatic Assistance and Methods for Accommodating Disaster Victims

Fundraising for the Flood Disaster: News continued to come in yesterday, including condolences from friendly nations Italy and Finland, the flight to Hankou by Zhu Qinglan and Zha Liangzhao, the resolution of accommodation methods, and the enthusiastic fundraising from all sectors. These are particularly important. Details are provided below:

Condolences from Italy and Finland Regarding the Flood Disaster in Our Country

According to the Shanghai office of the Italian Embassy, all sectors of the Italian government and public, upon learning of the severe flooding in various parts of our country, expressed deep sorrow. On the previous day, Italian Prime Minister Benito Mussolini, representing all sectors of the nation, sent a telegram to Italian Chargé d'Affaires in China, Cianno, instructing him to forward condolences to Chairman Chiang of the Nanjing National Government for all disaster areas in China. The original telegram was in Italian and was translated into Chinese yesterday (24th) by the Italian Chargé d'Affaires and forwarded to Chairman Zhuang of the Nanjing National Government to express condolences. The original telegram was translated into Chinese by Mr. Zhou Shuqing, secretary of the embassy, as follows: "To Chairman Chiang of the National Government of the Republic of China in Nanjing: Heaven has not blessed our friendly nation, which has suffered a terrible flood. The most prosperous provinces have become a watery expanse, with countless disaster victims everywhere. The alarming news has caused deep pain among government and public in our country. Therefore, the entire Fascist Italy extends its condolences to the people of our friendly nation. Please accept our sincere sympathies. Mussolini, Prime Minister of Italy, bows in respect." In addition, Finnish Chargé d'Affaires to China, Norlin, also recently received a telegram of condolence from the Finnish government to the National Government regarding the flood disaster. Mr. Norlin sealed the telegram in an envelope and personally delivered it to the Shanghai office of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs at Fenglin Bridge for forwarding to the National Government.

Relief Committee Discusses American Wheat Issue

The Finance Group of the National Flood Relief Committee met yesterday to discuss the telegram from the U.S. Department of Agriculture regarding the sale of wheat on credit. It is reported that further negotiations are needed with the Department regarding the repayment period and interest rates to obtain more favorable terms.

Zhu Qinglan and Others Scheduled to Fly to Hankou This Morning

Xu Shiying, Chairman of the Disaster Relief Committee, and Standing Committee member Qinglan, along with Zha Liangzhao and others from the North China Charity Federation, went to Song Ziwen's residence on Rue Bisson in the French Concession at 9 a.m. yesterday to discuss emergency relief measures for about an hour. Because of the severity of the disaster in various areas, Mr. Zhu believed that an on-site inspection was necessary to determine emergency relief measures. It was therefore decided that Mr. Zhu and Mr. Zha would take a flight to Hankou. The National Flood Relief Committee of the National Government will purchase airline tickets from China National Aviation Corporation for them. They are scheduled to depart from Longhua by plane at 7 a.m. today to inspect the situation along the way and plan to return to Shanghai by plane within two or three days. After investigating the disaster situation in various areas, they will begin to implement emergency relief measures.

Social Affairs Bureau Discussed Accommodation Measures Yesterday

Since receiving the order to plan for the accommodation of disaster victims, the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau immediately began to work. At 10 a.m. yesterday, letters were sent to the Public Safety and Health Bureaus and representatives of various organizations to discuss the matter. Those who attended included Director Hu of the Health Bureau and representatives of various organizations such as Wang Yiting, Huang Hanzhi, Wang Binyan, Ye Huijun, Wu Weide, and Xi Guansheng, totaling more than 30 people. Director Pan Gongzhan of the Social Affairs Bureau presided over the meeting and reported on the importance the municipal government attached to the flood disaster and the reason for convening the meeting. Director Hu then reported on the results of informal talks with the concessions, who were willing to do their utmost to assist. (1) It was decided to establish the Shanghai Disaster Victim Accommodation Office. (2) The office will have one director and four deputy directors. Wang Yiting was publicly elected as director, and Pan Gongzhan, Chen Xizeng, Hu Hongji, and Ye Huijun were elected as deputy directors. Five sections will be established: general affairs, supplies, health, security, and repatriation. Except for the security and health sections, which will be handled by personnel from the Public Safety and Health Bureaus, the remaining sections will be handled by the director and deputy directors. An office will be established in a convenient location. (3) The Disaster Relief Committee will send telegrams to the municipal governments of various provinces, instructing them to intercept and accommodate disaster victims who come down, with Shanghai only acting as a last resort. (4) Accommodation in this city will be based on the principle of centralization. If a large number of disaster victims arrive, it is planned to build houses on the vacant land of the Zhoujiazui Junpu Bureau for accommodation. The disaster victims currently arriving will be temporarily accommodated at the Chaozhou Villa in Nanshi and the gruel kitchen in Zhabei. (5) In addition to the funds allocated by the municipal government, assistance will be provided by various agencies, and no external donations will be solicited. (6) Feng Liutang, Shen Gao, and Jin Zhongjian were asked to draft the office's constitution. (7) Before the office's premises are determined, the Social Affairs Bureau will temporarily serve as the liaison office.

A Heartrending Telegram from the Hankou Chamber of Commerce

The Hubei Native Place Association in Shanghai's Emergency Relief Committee for the Flood Disaster in Hubei Province received a telegram from the Hankou Chamber of Commerce, which stated: "We believe that Hubei Province is the most severely affected by this great flood, and Wuhan is the most tragic. A prehistoric scene has reappeared, and a great calamity is at hand. The autumn waters stretch across the sky, and the disaster is not yet over. Because Hubei is located in the middle reaches of the Yangtze River, with the most lakes, it has always been known as a watery area. Wuchang and Xiaokou are at the confluence of the Han River. Therefore, there are floods every year, that is, floods every year. Since the beginning of summer this year, there have been continuous heavy rains, pouring down without stopping. Mountain floods have erupted, and canals and ponds have turned into turbid currents. On flat ground, wind and waves have accumulated into huge floods. The Guangyong River in Han and the Wu Gorge in Sichuan have waters ten feet high, flowing in the same direction. The counties along the river and lakes, which have always relied on embankments to protect their lives, number more than forty. The rushing currents have breached everything. Stone houses have boats on their roofs, and there is no way to travel on land. The dead are carried away by the currents, and no one asks about the fields. The living are like ants gathered on sandbars, in isolated circumstances. Alarming news is constantly being reported, which breaks the hearts of those who hear it. At this time, the members of our association, striving to follow the example of gentlemen from all walks of life, are organizing emergency relief and reinforcing river defenses, reducing food and clothing, hoping to be of some help. Unexpectedly, the surging forces are unstoppable. The Fenjinlu, Danshui Pond, and Dandongmen embankments, which the city of Hankou relied on for protection, have collapsed one after another, drowning countless people. Half of the wealth and property have been given to the floods. The depth is several feet in some places and several feet in others. There is water everywhere but no city life. There are boatmen but no pedestrians. All opportunities for life have been cut off. As for emergency relief, there are hundreds of thousands of disaster victims, and more than a hundred shelters are being relocated three times a day. As for disaster relief, all officials are disaster officials, and all people are disaster people. Disaster officials are saving disaster people, and the survivors are saving the dying. We dare not shirk our responsibility for surviving, but our efforts are like a cup of water trying to put out a cartload of burning wood, and our voices are hoarse and our strength is exhausted. The central government, mindful of the people's suffering, has recently allocated 170,000 yuan for relief. However, the total number of disaster victims in Hubei Province is nearly ten million. The daily cost of one meal of gruel per person is not cheap. Those waiting to be fed are crying out, 'We are hungry!' Moreover, Wuchang is following in Hankou's footsteps. There is no clean land to be seen. Alas, our children and grandchildren are facing endless calamities, burying themselves in mounds of earth, living as neighbors with ghosts, sleeping in the open air, exposed to wind and rain, suffering from hunger and cold. How can one reason with Heaven when life has reached this point? It is impossible for Zheng Xia's 'Refugee Pictures' to describe even one ten-thousandth of this situation. People call out to Heaven in times of urgent need, because Heaven has the virtue of cherishing life. People call out to their parents when they are sick, because parents have the sincerity of protecting their children. You gentlemen are either in charge of national affairs, or suppressing chaos and saving the people, or concerned about your hometowns, or helping each other in the same boat. We hope that you will show concern for the suffering of one person and give millions more bushels of unhusked rice. It is righteous to give what you have, not a favor. Carry rice and distribute it around. Do not complain about the labor of carts. Open granaries and provide relief. Do not wait to be punished in the capital. Contributing generously depends on benevolent people. Completing a fur coat depends on collecting from armpits. Saving one life is recognized by snakes and birds. Saving suffering in the three realms is jointly estimated by the gods. This is the Hankou Chamber of Commerce, on behalf of the ten million disaster victims who are on the verge of death, bowing a hundred times and calling out to Heaven and their parents, seeking immediate help from you gentlemen. The telegram is urgent and full of grief. Hankou Chamber of Commerce bows in respect."

Establishment of the Hubei Relief Office in Shanghai 102

The Hubei Flood Disaster Emergency Relief Association's Shanghai Relief Office held its inaugural meeting on the 23rd. Twelve people, including Liu Wanqing, attended the meeting as scheduled. Mr. Ming Runshen, a member of the committee, was publicly elected as temporary chairman. He reported on a telegram from the Hankou Hubei Flood Disaster Emergency Relief Association, which stated: "The disaster situation in our Hubei is extremely serious, and relief is urgently needed. It was decided at the tenth standing committee meeting of our association to establish a Shanghai Relief Office to rush to raise emergency relief funds to save the disaster victims." Jiang Yuyan was publicly elected as chairman of the committee, and eight standing committee members were appointed, divided into four sections: documentation, finance, publicity, and communication. They will begin work immediately. After the meeting adjourned, a telegram was sent to the Hankou Association reporting the progress of the inaugural meeting and requesting the Hankou Association to send a telegram to the Shanghai party and government agencies for the record to facilitate progress.

News from the Flood Disaster Committee in Various Provinces 103

The Flood Disaster Relief Committee of Various Provinces was convened yesterday (24th) by Wang Xiaolai and held a standing committee meeting at the Renji Hall. More than 20 people attended. Qin Runqing then reported that the money industry also had similar plans. Wu Zhihao then reported that the garment industry association had held a meeting and decided to contribute 10% of its business income for seven days to help the flood disaster. It also requested 30 donation books. Zhang Yichen reported that the Shanghai Special Municipal Citizens' Federation had convened all members of various branches and held a meeting at the General Chamber of Commerce. The fundraising methods were then discussed: (1) A proposal to widely invite fundraising committee members. (Resolution) All committee members of various labor unions and organizations will be hired as fundraising committee members. (2) A proposal to send letters to major companies to implement fundraising. (Resolution) Approved. (3) A proposal to request the Western Medical Association, etc., to start fundraising immediately. (Resolution) Send letters to the association, etc., to initiate fundraising. (4) How should the fundraising methods of various labor unions be determined? (Resolution) (A) Total recognition of a certain amount. (B) Contribute 5% to 10% of business income for a few days (e.g., seven days). (C) Free grouping for soliciting donations, such as 10 yuan per group, etc. Various companies can choose from the above three methods. (5) How to solicit donations from various churches? (Resolution) Send letters to various churches and have Mr. Weng Guoxun go to contact them separately. The meeting adjourned after the discussions.

Please reply. Sincerely, Qinglan." He also telegraphed Mr. Wang Younong at No. 16 Wangxing Bridge, Fengmennei, Suzhou: "I have sent a telegram. Please come to Shanghai today. Sincerely, Zhu Qinglan." I (25th) will take a plane to Hankou with Mianzhong in the morning to inspect the disaster situation. I will talk to you in person and please inform Mr. Ju Ke. Sincerely, Zhu Qinglan."

The Jiangsu Flood Disaster Relief Association has been working hard these days. It has been reported in this newspaper that the association has already issued donation books and is actively soliciting donations. The situation on the previous day is detailed below:

Cao Songqiao Arrives in Shanghai Cao Songqiao, the director of investigation and distribution of the association, is a great philanthropist from Suzhou. After receiving a telegram on the 22nd, he came to Shanghai to take care of everything and met with Zhu Qinglan. He then returned to Suzhou.

Donating Salaries for Relief Dai Buxiang, manager of the Great China Hotel in this city, and all employees voluntarily donated 437 yuan in salaries, which is commendable.

Disaster Reports from Various Counties (1) Jiangpu County: Since July, the county has experienced continuous heavy rains and floods. The floodwaters have not been able to be discharged, and the floodwaters from Huangshan in Quanjiao, Anhui, have passed through, causing the external waters to merge with the waters of this place, swelling and flowing horizontally, breaching more than ten dikes in the north and south districts. The remaining dikes along the river have burst, and the river tides have joined, causing water damage. The crops have rotted, and there is no hope of an autumn harvest. Most of the residents are in the water, and deaths have occurred one after another. The survivors have no place to live and no food to eat. Women are crying and children are weeping, and the scene is tragic. (2) Xinghua County: The county is surrounded by lakes and marshes and is originally a water town. This summer, continuous rain has caused disaster, and the river water has flowed horizontally, causing many dike banks in the countryside to collapse. The water in the city is extremely deep, reaching the chest. Since the opening of the Guanhai Three Dams, the entire county has become a watery expanse, and there is no hope of an autumn harvest. Wailing is heard everywhere, and the sight is distressing. The Dafeng and Yuhua dikes are obstructing the waterway and cannot flow smoothly into the sea, which is particularly worrying. It is now reported that gentry in Liuzhuang have telegraphed to request the opening of the Sanmaoyou River to discharge water to save the people's lives. (3) Bao Ying County: The county is located at the intersection of Xiang County and is low-lying, so it is always prone to flooding. A few months ago, there were continuous heavy rains, and the rivers and lakes rose together. The dikes in the west of the river have all collapsed, creating a vast expanse of water. The crops have been submerged, and people and animals have been washed away. The water level of the canal is higher than the people's houses, and the lakes and rivers are connected. Even with the addition of dikes, the water level is still rising and is in danger. Disaster victims have gathered here, from Huailou Bay in the south to Huangpu in the north, huddled together on mats and quilts, barely able to find space. (4) Gaoyou County: The county has suffered from drought for many years, and its vitality has been damaged. Since the beginning of summer, there has been excessive rainfall, and the Huai River has overflowed, causing the lake water to rise sharply. The dikes in the west of the lake have broken early, and the dikes in the east of the lake are also in danger. There are leaks in the gates everywhere. Therefore, the ditches in the lower reaches have long been full, and with the addition of the lake roaring and the three dams opening at the same time, a vast expanse of water has been created. The crops have been submerged, and the houses have been swept away. The young and strong are standing on the treetops, and the cries for help are louder than the morning market. The cries shake the sky, and it is heartbreaking to hear. (5) Huai'an County: The county has suffered from disasters for the past three years. This summer, there has been continuous rainfall, and the Huai River has risen sharply. The banks of the city river were the first to be flooded. The areas around Xunhe in the west of the county and the fields in the sixth and seventh fang and half of the fifth fang and half of the area have all been submerged one after another, creating a vast expanse of water with only the tops of trees showing. Many houses have been submerged, and tens of thousands of disaster victims are crying out to the heavens. They are now living on the Honghu Dam, the Wanji River Dam, and the Xinhe River Dams, waiting to be fed, and the situation is very dangerous. (6) Tongshan County: The county is adjacent to the coast, and the people are mostly poor and work hard all year round, with little savings. Last month, the rain did not stop, and the water from the sky poured down, flooding both inside and outside the city, with the water reaching the chest in some places and the knees in others. The water level in the old Yellow River outside the northeast city has increased sharply, and the bridges have collapsed. The river dikes have been in disrepair for many years, and the water is about to pour in, causing panic. The poor families along the roads have lost their shacks and barely saved their lives, sleeping in the open air, exposed to wind and rain, which is very pitiful.

Jisheng Association Handles Emergency Relief in Wuhan 108

The Chinese Jisheng Association and the Shanghai Flood Disaster Relief Association of Various Provinces publicly nominated Zhu Qichen, a standing committee member of the Jisheng Association, to take the Fengyang Maru steamship with experienced relief workers on the 22nd, carrying relief funds and 10,000 bags of flour, including 5,000 bags from Wang Junwei of the Lianyi Charity Association, and tens of thousands of bottles of relief medicine to Wuhan to investigate and provide emergency relief. Several methods for handling the disaster-stricken areas in Wuhan were also proposed. The details are listed below:

General Principles Military and police protection, sealing the barges, providing workers with food every day, building sheds in Hanyang Guishan Black Mountain as shelters, each shed accommodating about 100 people, building sheds in Wuchang Snake Mountain Hongshan as shelters, each shed accommodating about 100 people, setting up temporary medical rooms in the health department, which will be handled by the director of the medical department, preparing a large ship as the headquarters for the relief workers, with a temporary clinic attached, and another ship for storing relief grain and necessary items, beverages, coal, etc., and another ship specifically for transporting refugees from downstream ports to Shanghai and back to the disaster area. The above ships can be added, and the support of doctors and medicines on board should be borne by the director of the medical department. The directors of each port barge are responsible for loading refugees, such as unloading or needing to load items, and should contact them in advance. (Temporary Rescue Methods) (1) Organize rescue barges, with ten in each group, numbered and marked with flags during the day and mast lights at night to make it easier for refugees to identify them. (2) Each group is divided into districts for rescue. (3) Rescue disaster victims gathered on high embankments. Due to the large number of people and the variety of categories, there must be competition and risks to the rescue work. Therefore, each boat must have armed military police to announce to the refugees that a certain barge can only accommodate a certain number of people, and several people are elected from the disaster victims to help greet them. The refugees board the boat in order and cross to Hanyang as the first step. After the Hanyang shelter is full, they are transported to Wuchang. Wuchang has a wider river surface, which takes too long. Therefore, they first go to Hanyang, which is closer, so that more people can be rescued. If there are bad people who deliberately disrupt the work, they should be stopped with police force. (4) Patrol rescue teams are specialized in rescuing refugees trapped in houses by water. Ask them how many people want to go to the shelter or which port they want to go to downstream, and let them do as they please, and the team will transport them. If the person does not want to leave the house, they should be shown the advantages and disadvantages. If they still do not want to leave, they should be given the necessary items. (5) It is easier to help refugees who want to be given a few yuan or some dry food to make a living on their own. (6) Use clean drinking water groups to provide the water needed in the shelter and the drinking water for the refugees in the houses. (General Affairs Section) To lead the entire department, it is divided into a director of general affairs, a secretary, a clerk, an accountant, a liaison officer, a receiver, a dispatcher, and miscellaneous staff, as well as all kinds of miscellaneous affairs. (Shipping Department) The shipping department is divided into a director, who is responsible for the arrival and departure of ships in Hankou and the distribution of barges, and is ordered by the General Affairs Department. (Rescue Department) The rescue department is divided into a director and several rescuers. The required ships or swift ships and military police are all contacted by the General Affairs Department and issued by the Shipping Department. (Accommodation Department) The accommodation department is divided into a director, a manager, a register of disaster victims, and a miscellaneous staff. What is needed is issued by the General Affairs Department and taken from each department, registered, and reported. (Medical Department) The medical department is divided into a director, a doctor, a pharmacist, and a relief worker, who are responsible for temporary hospital duties, inspecting the bodies of the refugees in the shelter to see if they are complete, and transporting them downstream. A doctor and medicine should be sent with the ship to be distributed. (Relief Department) The relief department is divided into a director and a relief worker who are responsible for distributing the food needed by the disaster victims in the disaster area and the food and clothing needed in the shelter. How much relief supplies are needed every day? The director will calculate the approximate amount a day in advance and take it from the relief supplies management department. (Relief Supplies Management and Transportation Department) There is a director in charge of extracting and issuing the arrival of relief supplies in Hankou and registering them. (Economic Department) There is a director in charge of the money. The General Affairs Department will pay it according to the payment slip. If it is affiliated to a relief organization, there will be an economic officer in charge, and it is not included in this list. (Compilation Department) A director is responsible for compiling the disaster situation and the rescue process to commemorate it and show credibility. The above organization and management are complex and different. It is necessary to go to Wuhan to negotiate with the local charitable organizations to work together. Employees are obliged to temporarily agree on the method of requesting various companies to send the train or the small wheel back to the refugees for free or by subsidizing the expenses, and the situation must be reviewed and handled on the spot. The disaster areas in Hanyang, Wuchang, Xujiapeng, Yingzhou, Baishazhou, Liujiamiao, Danshui Pond, etc. must also be inspected on the spot to determine the relief policy.

Fan Chang's Xu Yangwo Arrives in Shanghai to Appeal for Help 111

Fan Chang, located upstream of Wuhu, borders the river and has many polder fields. In recent years, it has suffered from repeated banditry, and the people are destitute. This year, it has suffered from a major flood, and all the dikes in the four rural areas have been almost completely washed away. It is estimated that over 190,000 acres of farmland have been flooded, and the disaster has affected over 200,000 people. They are emaciated and miserable. The disaster is unusually severe and unprecedented in a century. Although a flood relief committee has been organized by various sectors to solicit donations, the disaster area is too large and difficult to provide universal relief. Mr. Xu Yangwo was sent to Shanghai to appeal to the Anhui Flood Relief Association of Shanghai, the China International Famine Relief Commission, the Shanghai Fund-Raising Committee for Emergency Relief in Various Provinces, the Shanghai Jisheng Society, the National Government Flood Emergency Relief Committee, the National Red Cross Society, and various charitable organizations, working tirelessly and enduring great hardships.

Wang Yiting and Others Hold Flood Disaster Prayer Meeting 112

Philanthropists Wang Yiting, Xu Shiying, Wang Xiaoyu, Xu Guannan, Weng Yinchu, and the president of the Bodhi Dharma Assembly, Qinghai Peng, and other monks, initiated a grand prayer meeting for the flood disaster to pray for divine harmony and eliminate the disaster. Shao Ruxin and Weng Ruiwu and others sent letters to various celebrities and philanthropists to participate in the prayer, sincerely seeking help. The association is scheduled to hold the altar at the Qingliang Temple in the Xin Family Garden on Xinzha Road on the evening of the 25th of the eighth month of the lunar calendar (August 25th of the Western calendar), starting chanting sutras on the morning of the 26th, offering vegetarian meals and submitting petitions on the afternoon of the 27th, and completing the Buddhist service on the 28th, and observing a three-day fast during the period.

Bank of China Donates a Large Sum Again: The Bank of China previously deducted donations from the salaries of its employees, totaling 20,000 yuan, which was delivered to the Shanghai Fund-Raising Committee for Flood Relief in Various Provinces on the 22nd. Now, all employees of the bank's branches across the country and the Shanghai head office have voluntarily donated another 100,000 yuan.

The staff of the Bank of Communications spontaneously initiated a donation from their salaries to assist in disaster relief. Wing On Company Donates 20,000 Yuan: The Wing On Company donated 20,000 yuan to assist in relief efforts.

Pudong Electric Company Employees Donate Salaries: The employees of the Pudong Electric Company agreed to donate their August salaries to the relief effort. The company will advance the funds first and then deduct them in installments according to the following standards: (1) Those with a monthly salary of 150 yuan or more will donate the full amount and have it deducted in five months. (2) Those with a monthly salary of 120 yuan or more will donate four-fifths of the amount and have it deducted in four months. (3) Those with a monthly salary of 90 yuan or more will donate three-fifths of the amount and have it deducted in three months. (4) Those with a monthly salary of 60 yuan or more will donate two-fifths of the amount and have it deducted in two months. (5) Those with a monthly salary of less than 60 yuan will donate one-fifth of the amount, which will be deducted in one installment at the end of this month. The funds for the Mid-Autumn Festival and year-end banquets for all employees will also be transferred to the donation, totaling 1,003 yuan, which was delivered to the Bank of China yesterday.

Customs Brokers Raise Donations for Disaster Relief: Customs broker leaders Shi Zhikun, You Senting, and others have specially solicited donations from their colleagues for disaster relief. They have issued a prospectus yesterday.

Wuzhou Pharmacy Branch Reduces Food to Assist in Relief: The staff of the Wuzhou Second Branch on North Sichuan Road, in addition to donating one-tenth of their salaries, will also reduce their food intake for one month, totaling 50 yuan, which will be delivered to the Flood Relief Committee for Various Provinces.

Youzheng Bookstore Sells at Low Prices to Assist in Relief: From the 25th, Youzheng Bookstore will use three days of sales proceeds, including the principal, to assist in flood relief.

Yuanyuan Company Employees Donate Salaries to Assist in Relief: Yesterday, the employees of the Yuanyuan Weaving Company's distribution office and factory decided to spontaneously initiate a disaster relief association. From the assistant manager down, everyone is willing to donate 10% of their monthly labor income to Qingjiang to provide relief to the disaster victims.

The general office will be located at the Central Movie Company at 35 Renji Road to facilitate centralized coordination.
